   "source": [
    "# Game of life\n",
    "\n",
    "adaptiert von: https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/conways-game-life-python-implementation/\n",
    "\n",
    "* ArgParser entfernt\n",
    "* update-Methode in updateGrids und updateAnimation aufgeteilt\n",
    "    * updateAnimation zeigt das initiale Grid für den ersten Frame an\n",
    "* verschiedene initiale Grids\n",
    "* Animationen für mehrere Grids\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "## Anmerkung\n",
    "Wenn die Videos nicht angezeigt werden sollten, können folgende Anaconda-Pakte installiert werden (entweder über den *Anaconda Navigator -> CMD.exe Prompt* oder über *JupyterLab -> File -> New -> Terminal*)\n",
    "* `conda install -c conda-forge ffmpeg`\n",
    "* `conda install -c conda-forge ipympl`"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## Methodendefinition"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 1,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "# Python code to implement Conway's Game Of Life\n",
    "\n",
    "import numpy as np\n",
    "import matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n",
    "import matplotlib.animation as animation\n",
    "from matplotlib import rc\n",
    "\n",
    "# setting up the values for the grid\n",
    "ON = 255\n",
    "OFF = 0\n",
    "vals = [ON, OFF]\n",
    "\n",
    "rc('animation', html='html5')   # Animationen rendern nun in HTML (für JupyterLab nötig)\n",
    "\n",
    "def randomGrid(N):\n",
    "\n",
    "    \"\"\"returns a grid of NxN random values\"\"\"\n",
    "    return np.random.choice(vals, N*N, p=[0.15, 0.85]).reshape(N, N)\n",
    "\n",
    "def addGlider(i, j, grid):\n",
    "\n",
    "    \"\"\"adds a glider with top left cell at (i, j)\"\"\"\n",
    "    glider = np.array([[0, 0, 255],\n",
    "                    [255, 0, 255],\n",
    "                    [0, 255, 255]])\n",
    "    grid[i:i+3, j:j+3] = glider\n",
    "\n",
    "def addGosperGliderGun(i, j, grid):\n",
    "\n",
    "    \"\"\"adds a Gosper Glider Gun with top left\n",
    "    cell at (i, j)\"\"\"\n",
    "    gun = np.zeros(11*38).reshape(11, 38)\n",
    "\n",
    "    gun[5][1] = gun[5][2] = 255\n",
    "    gun[6][1] = gun[6][2] = 255\n",
    "\n",
    "    gun[3][13] = gun[3][14] = 255\n",
    "    gun[4][12] = gun[4][16] = 255\n",
    "    gun[5][11] = gun[5][17] = 255\n",
    "    gun[6][11] = gun[6][15] = gun[6][17] = gun[6][18] = 255\n",
    "    gun[7][11] = gun[7][17] = 255\n",
    "    gun[8][12] = gun[8][16] = 255\n",
    "    gun[9][13] = gun[9][14] = 255\n",
    "\n",
    "    gun[1][25] = 255\n",
    "    gun[2][23] = gun[2][25] = 255\n",
    "    gun[3][21] = gun[3][22] = 255\n",
    "    gun[4][21] = gun[4][22] = 255\n",
    "    gun[5][21] = gun[5][22] = 255\n",
    "    gun[6][23] = gun[6][25] = 255\n",
    "    gun[7][25] = 255\n",
    "\n",
    "    gun[3][35] = gun[3][36] = 255\n",
    "    gun[4][35] = gun[4][36] = 255\n",
    "\n",
    "    grid[i:i+11, j:j+38] = gun\n",
    "\n",
    "def updateGrid(grid, N):\n",
    "    newGrid = grid.copy()\n",
    "    for i in range(N):\n",
    "        for j in range(N):\n",
    "\n",
    "            # compute 8-neighbor sum\n",
    "            # using toroidal boundary conditions - x and y wrap around\n",
    "            # so that the simulaton takes place on a toroidal surface.\n",
    "            total = int((grid[i, (j-1)%N] + grid[i, (j+1)%N] +\n",
    "                        grid[(i-1)%N, j] + grid[(i+1)%N, j] +\n",
    "                        grid[(i-1)%N, (j-1)%N] + grid[(i-1)%N, (j+1)%N] +\n",
    "                        grid[(i+1)%N, (j-1)%N] + grid[(i+1)%N, (j+1)%N])/255)\n",
    "\n",
    "            # apply Conway's rules\n",
    "            if grid[i, j] == ON:\n",
    "                if (total < 2) or (total > 3):\n",
    "                    newGrid[i, j] = OFF\n",
    "            else:\n",
    "                if total == 3:\n",
    "                    newGrid[i, j] = ON\n",
    "    return newGrid\n",
    "\n",
    "def updateAnimation(frameNum, img, grid, N):\n",
    "\n",
    "    if frameNum == 0:                # include initial image in animation\n",
    "        return img,\n",
    "    # copy grid since we require 8 neighbors\n",
    "    # for calculation and we go line by line\n",
    "    newGrid = updateGrid(grid,N)\n",
    "\n",
    "    # update data\n",
    "    img.set_data(newGrid)\n",
    "    grid[:] = newGrid[:]\n",
    "    return img,\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "def createGrid(N, type = \"random\"):\n",
    "    grid = np.array([])\n",
    "\n",
    "    # glider = False\n",
    "    # gosper = False\n",
    "\n",
    "    # check if \"glider\" demo flag is specified\n",
    "    if type == \"glider\":\n",
    "        grid = np.zeros(N*N).reshape(N, N)\n",
    "        addGlider(1, 1, grid)\n",
    "    elif  type == \"gosper\":\n",
    "        grid = np.zeros(N*N).reshape(N, N)\n",
    "        addGosperGliderGun(10, 10, grid)\n",
    "\n",
    "    else: # populate grid with random on/off -\n",
    "            # more off than on\n",
    "        grid = randomGrid(N)\n",
    "    return grid \n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "\n"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},

    "plt.rcParams[\"figure.figsize\"] = (20,4) #resize figures\n",
    "\n",
    "# set grid size\n",
    "\n",
    "N = 50\n",
    "grid = createGrid(N, )\n",
    "fig, (ax1, ax2, ax3, ax4, ax5) = plt.subplots(1, 5)\n",
    "fig.suptitle('Random grid')\n",
    "img = ax1.imshow(grid, interpolation='nearest')\n",
    "grid = updateGrid(grid,N)\n",
    "img = ax2.imshow(grid, interpolation='nearest')\n",
    "grid = updateGrid(grid,N)\n",

    "N = 25\n",
    "updateInterval= 250    # frameRate in ms\n",
    "grid = createGrid(N )\n",

    "# create gosper grid\n",
    "N = 50\n",
    "updateInterval= 250    # frameRate in ms\n",
    "grid = createGrid(N, 'gosper' )\n",
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# set up animation\n",
    "fig, ax = plt.subplots()\n",
    "img = ax.imshow(grid, interpolation='nearest')\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.close()\n",
    "\n",
    "ani = animation.FuncAnimation(fig, updateAnimation, fargs=(img, grid, N, ),\n",
    "                            frames = 100,\n",
    "                            interval=updateInterval, blit=True)\n",
